</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Symphonies&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Symphonies</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For orchestra</a></span>; <div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Symphony No.2
</td></tr>

<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
